6/8/20, 2:42 pm - Erick Hernandez: #include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

struct reservacion {
	int numero_vuelo;
	char aeropuerto [4];
	char aeropuerto_ida[4];
	char tiempo_vuelo[16];
	char time_llegada[16];
};

int main(void) {

	char aeropuerto1[100];         
	char aeropuerto2[100];         

	int i;                      

	struct reservacion reservations[20] = { 
		{ 2273, "CMX", "MID", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" },
		{ 9912, "MID", "CMX", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" },
		{ 231,  "CAM", "HGO", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" },
		{ 444,  "CMX", "GTO", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" },
		{ 9823, "MID", "HGO", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" },
		{ 1541, "CMX", "MTY", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" },
		{ 5812, "CMX", "GRO", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" },
		{ 7213, "CMX", "VER", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" },
		{ 1312, "CMX", "SLP", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" },
		{ 2145, "MID", "BJS", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" },
		{ 421, "MTY", "BJN", "08062020227321", "08062020227321" }
	};
	printf("Aeropuertos disponibles:\n");
	printf("\nCMX=Ciudad de Mexico, MID=Merida, CAM=Campeche, MTY= Monterrey\n");
	printf("\n");
	
	
	printf("Ingresa el codigo de un aeropuerto: ");
	fgets(aeropuerto1, sizeof(aeropuerto1), stdin);
	aeropuerto1[strlen(aeropuerto1) - 1] = '\0';          

	printf("Ingresa el codigo de otro aeropuerto: ");
	fgets(aeropuerto2, sizeof(aeropuerto2), stdin);
	aeropuerto2[strlen(aeropuerto2) - 1] = '\0';          

	for (i = 0; i < sizeof(reservations); ++i) {
		if ((strncmp(reservations[i].aeropuerto, aeropuerto1, sizeof(aeropuerto1)) == 0) ||
			(strncmp(reservations[i].aeropuerto, aeropuerto2, sizeof(aeropuerto2)) == 0)) {
					printf("Found flight %d: %s -> %s\n", reservations[i].numero_vuelo,
							reservations[i].aeropuerto, reservations[i].aeropuerto_ida);
		}
	}

	return(0);

}
